1
(8)*((log(8*x))^2)
4
8*x

Check:
check

Output:
1 int
2 de
M: f: 1 auto
2 dir
3 trig
4 sub
5 pts
6 pf
7 div
Met: u: Method: Integration by parts
1. u = ln(x)^2
2. du/dx = 2*ln(x)/x
3. v = 8*x/ln(8)^2
4. I = u*v-Int[16*ln(x)/ln(8)^2] dx
5. Now integrate Int[16*ln(x)/ln(8)^2] dx
6. u = ln(x)
7. du/dx = 1/x
8. du = 1/x dx
9. I = Int[16*u*e^u/ln(8)^2] du
10. = 16*u*e^u/ln(8)^2-16*e^u/ln(8)^2 + C
11. = 16*ln(x)*x/ln(8)^2-16*x/ln(8)^2 + C
12. = 8*ln(x)^2*x/ln(8)^2-16*ln(x)*x/ln(8)^2+16*x/ln(8)^2 + C

Met: u: Method: Integration by parts

4. I = Int[e^u] du
5. = e^u + C
